parts.push(`<strong>${summary.unresolved_exceptions}</strong> unresolved exceptions`);\n724\t            }\n725\t\n726\t            if (parts.length > 0) {\n727\t                el.innerHTML = '📊   }\n733\t\n734\t        async function registerSurface() {\n735\t            try {\n736\t                const response = await fetch('/api/v1/surfaces/register', {\n737\t                    method: DB/result independent —\n758\t        // the welcome card renders even against an empty component store. Its project list + example\n792\t                // utterances come from the registry (never the DB), so we only\n793\t                // need to fetch it on the zero-card branch. The welcome card is\n794\t                // dropped — not duplicated — the moment the first real result\n795\t                // lands: the next SSE result_created → loadTopics() reload\n796\t                // yields a non-empty card set, so buildContainerChildren()\n797\t                // returns topic cards only (clearing the welcome card).\n798\t                const projects = cards.length ? }\n808\t\n809\t        function connectSSE() {\n810\t            updateConnectionStatus('connecting', 'Connecting...');\n811\t\n812\t            const url = };\n819\t\n820\t            eventSource.onerror = (error) => {\n821\t                console.error('SSE error:', error);\n822\t                updateConnectionStatus('disconnected', <div style=\"display:flex;align-items:baseline;gap:8px\">\n                <h1>ADC Canvas</h1>\n                <span id=\"versionBadge\"      </svg>\n            </button>\n        </div>\n\n        <div id=\"topicsContainer\" class=\"topics-grid\">\n            <div class=\"loading\">\n                <div class=\"spinner\"></div>\n                <span>Loading topics...</span>\n            </div>\n        </div>\n    </div>\n\n    <!-- Render helpers (createTopicCard + friends) — loaded before the app\n         script so they're available as globals and unit-testable headlessly. -->\n    <script src=\"/canvas.js\"></script>\n    <script>\n        // Session and surface IDs from URL params or generate new\n        const urlParams = new URLSearchParams(window.location.search);\n        const sessionId = urlParams.get('session_id') || generateId();\n        const surfaceType = 'canvas';\n\n        let surfaceId = null;\n        let eventSource = null;\n\n        // Track pending placeholders so we can find/replace them later.\n        // Key: pendingId (utterance_id), Value: placeholder HTMLElement.\n        var pendingPlaceholders = {};\n\n        // Update URL with session_id for reload persistence\n        if (!urlParams.get('session_id')) {\n            urlParams.set('session_id', sessionId);\n            window.history.replaceState({}, '', `${window.location.pathname}?${urlParams}`);\n        }\n\n        function generateId() {\n            return 'adc-' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 16);\n        }\n\n        // createTopicCard / escapeHtml / formatStaleness / getStalenessLevel live\n        // in /canvas.js (loaded below as a blocking <script src> before this\n        // block), so they are available as globals here and unit-testable\n        // headlessly. See src/canvas/canvas.js.\n\n        function updateConnectionStatus(status, text) {\n            const dot = document.getElementById('statusDot');\n            const statusText = document.getElementById('statusText');\n\n            dot.className = 'status-dot ' + status;\n            statusText.textContent = text;\n        }\n\n        function showWorkloadSummary(summary) {\n            const el = document.getElementById('workloadSummary');\n            const parts = [];\n\n            if (summary.pending_intents > 0) {\n                parts.push(`<strong>${summary.pending_intents}</strong> pending intents`);\n            }\n            if (summary.new_results > 0) {\n                parts.push(`<strong>${summary.new_results}</strong> new results`);\n            }\n            if (summary.unresolved_exceptions > 0) {\n                parts.push(`<strong>${summary.unresolved_exceptions}</strong> unresolved exceptions`);\n            }\n\n            if (parts.length > 0) {\n                el.innerHTML = '📊 While you were away: ' + parts.join(', ');\n                el.classList.add('show');\n            } else {\n                el.classList.remove('show');\n            }\n        }\n\n        async function registerSurface() {\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch('/api/v1/surfaces/register', {\n                    method: 'POST',\n                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n                    body: JSON.stringify({\n                        session_id: sessionId,\n                        surface_type: surfaceType\n                    })\n                });\n\n                if (!response.ok) throw new Error('Failed to register surface');\n\n                const data = await response.json();\n                surfaceId = data.surface_id;\n                return surfaceId;\n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error('Error registering surface:', error);\n                throw error;\n            }\n        }\n\n        // Registry project list for the first-run welcome card\n        // (config/registry.yaml → GET /api/v1/registry). DB/result independent —\n        // the welcome card renders even against an empty component store. Cached\n        // after the first fetch so the per-SSE-event reloads don't refetch it.\n        let welcomeProjects = null;\n\n        async function loadWelcomeProjects() {\n            if (welcomeProjects) return welcomeProjects;\n            try {\n                const resp = await fetch('/api/v1/registry');\n                if (resp.ok) {\n                    const data = await resp.json();\n                    welcomeProjects = (data && data.projects) || [];\n                    return welcomeProjects;\n                }\n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error('Error loading registry for welcome card:', error);\n            }\n            // Graceful fallback: an empty list still renders the welcome card\n            // (with default example utterances), so a wedged registry endpoint\n            // never leaves the canvas bare.\n            welcomeProjects = [];\n            return welcomeProjects;\n        }\n\n        async function loadTopics() {\n            try {\n                const response = await fetch(`/api/v1/sessions/${sessionId}/topics`);\n                if (!response.ok) return;\n\n                const data = await response.json();\n                const container = document.getElementById('topicsContainer');\n                const cards = data.cards || [];\n\n                // Fresh session (zero topics): show the first-run welcome card\n                // instead of the bare empty-state. Its project list + example\n                // utterances come from the registry (never the DB), so we only\n                // need to fetch it on the zero-card branch. The welcome card is\n                // dropped — not duplicated — the moment the first real result\n                // lands: the next SSE result_created → loadTopics() reload\n                // yields a non-empty card set, so buildContainerChildren()\n                // returns topic cards only (clearing the welcome card).\n                const projects = cards.length ? [] : await loadWelcomeProjects();\n\n                container.innerHTML = '';\n                buildContainerChildren(cards, projects).forEach(node => {\n                    container.appendChild(node);\n                });\n            } catch (error) {\n                console.error('Error loading topics:', error);\n            }\n        }\n\n        function connectSSE() {\n            updateConnectionStatus('connecting', 'Connecting...');\n\n            const url = `/api/v1/sse?surface_id=${encodeURIComponent(surfaceId)}&session_id=${encodeURIComponent(sessionId)}&surface_type=${encodeURIComponent(surfaceType)}`;\n            eventSource = new EventSource(url);\n\n            eventSource.onopen = () => {\n                updateConnectionStatus('', 'Connected');\n                loadTopics();\n            };\n\n            eventSource.onerror = (error) => {\n                console.error('SSE error:', error);\n                updateConnectionStatus('disconnected', 'Disconnected');\n            };\n\n            eventSource.addEventListener('connected', (event) => {\n                const data = JSON.parse(event.data);\n                console.log('SSE connected:', data);\n            });\n\n            eventSource.addEventListener('workload_summary', (event) => {\n                const summary = JSON.parse(event.data);\n                showWorkloadSummary(summary);\n            });\n\n            // Dispatch ack: backup path for intent_ids if the fetch response didn't\n            // include them (e.g., the response arrived before the intent was routed).\n            eventSource.addEventListener('dispatch_ack', (event) => {\n                const data = JSON.parse(event.data);\n                const utteranceId = data.utterance_id;\n                const intentIds = data.intent_ids;\n                const utterance = data.utterance;\n\n                if (!utteranceId || !intentIds || !Array.isArray(intentIds)) return;\n\n                // Check if there's an existing placeholder to split\n                const placeholder = pendingPlaceholders[utteranceId];\n                const createdAt = placeholder\n                    ? parseInt(placeholder.dataset.createdAt, 10)\n                    : Date.now();\n\n                // Split into per-thread pending cards\n                const threadCards = splitPlaceholderToThreads(utterance, createdAt, intentIds);\n\n                const container = document.getElementById('topicsContainer');\n\n                if (placeholder && placeholder.parentNode) {\n                    // Replace the placeholder with the thread cards\n                    const frag = document.createDocumentFragment();\n                    threadCards.forEach(function (c) { frag.appendChild(c); });\n                    placeholder.parentNode.replaceChild(frag, placeholder);\n                } else {\n                    // No placeholder (test scenario or race condition): prepend thread cards\n                    const frag = document.createDocumentFragment();\n                    threadCards.forEach(function (c) { frag.appendChild(c); });\n                    container.insertBefore(frag, container.firstChild);\n                }\n\n                // No longer track this placeholder\n                delete pendingPlaceholders[utteranceId];\n            });\n\n            // Per-source progress update for a thread\n            eventSource.addEventListener('progress_update', (event) => {\n                const data = JSON.parse(event.data);\n                const intentId = data.intent_id;\n                const completed = data.completed;\n                const total = data.total;\n\n                if (!intentId) return;\n\n                // Find the pending thread card by intent_id\n                const threadCard = document.querySelector('[data-pending-id=\"' + intentId + '\"]');\n                if (!threadCard) {\n                    console.warn('progress_update: threadCard is null for intent_id=' + intentId);\n                    return;\n                }\n                if (!threadCard.classList.contains('pending-card')) {\n                    console.warn('progress_update: threadCard does not have pending-card class for intent_id=' + intentId);\n                    return;\n                }\n                if (typeof _setProgress !== 'function') {\n                    console.warn('progress_update: _setProgress is not a function');\n                    return;\n                }\n                _setProgress(threadCard, { completed: completed, total: total });\n            });\n\n            eventSource.addEventListener('result_created', (event) => {\n                const result = JSON.parse(event.data);\n                console.log('New result:', result);\n                loadTopics(); // Reload topics to show new result\n            });\n\n            eventSource.addEventListener('topic_updated', (event) => {\n                const topic = JSON.parse(event.data);\n                console.log('Topic updated:', topic);\n                loadTopics();\n            });\n\n            eventSource.addEventListener('disconnect', (event) => {\n                const data = JSON.parse(event.data);\n                console.log('Server disconnect:', data);\n                updateConnectionStatus('disconnected', 'Disconnected');\n                eventSource.close();\n            });\n        }\n\n        // Elapsed-time ticker for pending cards\n        // Every second, update the elapsed-time footer on all pending cards\n        // and apply aged treatment if they've exceeded the 30s threshold.\n        setInterval(function () {\n            var now = Date.now();\n            var pendingCards = document.querySelectorAll('.pending-card[data-pending-id]');\n            pendingCards.forEach(function (card) {\n                tickPendingElapsed(card, now);\n                applyAgedTreatment(card, now);\n            });\n        }, 1000);\n\n        // Heartbeat to keep surface alive\n        setInterval(() => {\n            if (surfaceId) {\n                fetch('/api/v1/surfaces/heartbeat', {\n                    method: 'POST',\n                    headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' },\n                    body: JSON.stringify({\n                        surface_id: surfaceId,\n                        session_id: sessionId\n                    })\n                }).catch(console.error);\n            }\n        }, 30000); // Every 30 seconds\n\n        // ── Input bar ──────────────────────────────────────────────────────────\n\n        const textarea = document.getElementById('inputTextarea');\n        const btnSend  = document.getElementById('btnSend');\n        const btnMic   = document.getElementById('btnMic');\n\n        // Auto-resize textarea\n        textarea.addEventListener('input', () => {\n            textarea.style.height = 'auto';\n            textarea.style.height = Math.min(textarea.scrollHeight, 160) + 'px';\n            btnSend.disabled = textarea.value.trim().length === 0;\n        });\n\n        // Send on Enter (Shift+Enter = newline)\n        textarea.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {\n            if (e.key === 'Enter' && !e.shiftKey) {\n                e.preventDefault();\n                if (!btnSend.disabled) dispatch(textarea.value.trim());\n            }\n        });\n\n        btnSend.addEventListener('click', () => {\n            if (!btnSend.disabled) dispatch(textarea.value.trim());\n        });\n\n        async function dispatch(utterance) {\n            if (!utterance) return;\n            textarea.value = '';\n            textarea.style.height = 'auto';\n            btnSend.disabled = true;\n\n            // Generate a client-side pending ID for the placeholder. We'll swap it\n            // for the server's utterance_id when the response arrives.\n            var pendingId = 'pending-' + Date.now() + '-' + Math.random().toString(36).substr(2, 8);\n            var createdAt = Date.now();\n\n            // Create the pending placeholder NOW, before the server round-trip,\n            // so a hung server still leaves a card on canvas to age.\n            var
